#stc14 ... meet @raygallon again Thought Leader ADOBE webinar "4x Series: Tech Challenges: Surfing and Diving Deep" http://t.co/WxiW8xTfdJ
@raygallon #stc14 This VIRTUOUS CIRCLE is a SHARING CIRCLE with all STAKE HOLDERS
@raygallon #stc14 Use STORYTELLING: in User Assistance tell your learning story -- ASK YOUR USERS to tell their stories
@raygallon #stc14 Ask OPEN QUESTIONS in your USER ASSISTANCE ... don't provide the answer ... encouraging users to collaborate/consensus
@raygallon #stc14 Gamification doesn't work well for reputation (like Kout and LinkedIn endorsements). Reward REAL accomplishments
@raygallon #stc14 GAMIFYING BEHAVIOUR: build loyalty, gain mastery, aid quality and build engagement
@raygallon #stc14 "FAQs are solutions in search of problems"
@raygallon #stc14 Publish your solutions, and get a hashtag to identify them. Post solutions on a scheduled basis
@raygallon #stc14 Be courageous: failure is a learning experience. "Never trust anybody who hasn't had a disaster" Fail early / Fail often
@raygallon #stc14 Collect failure. If you don't, the social nets will.
@raygallon #stc14 Crowd-source the pain points amongst your customers
@raygallon #stc14 Appeal to user's emotions and self-satisfaction. If they feel good during consumption, they will feel good about us.
@raygallon #stc14 Ways to get there ... self-diagnosis. Give people tools to do this; tools to get out of trouble. Users get distracted
@raygallon #stc14 Reflect and evaluate the Content ... the refelct on and evaluate the Message
